Without saying much, I continue to scroll down and see Xiangsheng. Xiangsheng also has a place in Putuo Mountain. I have stayed there and it feels good. Click in and find the target room. It is more than two levels higher than the hotel that squeezed in six or seven hundred to eat on the street beach two days ago.
Xiangsheng is the hotel I am most satisfied with since the holiday travel after the epidemic. It is luxurious, high-quality, honest and trustworthy. I highly recommend it and thank Ctrip for providing this high-quality option.
